OUR STORY

Science First.
Built on the Sand.

KARTER BORO 3.3 · PHASE B ACTIVES
THE PROCESS

"Science first. Marketing second. Always."

Fifteen-plus years in medical sales, pharma, and biologics — including surgical case support in operating rooms — shaped how every formula was built. Not like a hobbyist experimenting in a kitchen. Like a science professional who understands exactly how biological systems work.

THE ORIGIN

Science first.
Always.

Before St. Pete Tallow existed, there were 15+ years in medical sales, pharmaceutical science, and medical device — including regenerative biologics case support in operating rooms. Wellness, science, and human biology have never been abstract concepts. They have been the foundation of a career.

That background does not leave you when you walk off the court. It changes how you think about everything — including what you put on your skin.

The problem was simple and familiar to anyone who trains and competes outside. Every moisturizer evaporated before noon. Water-based lotions that felt hydrating for 20 minutes, then left skin drier than before. Products engineered for a climate-controlled bathroom, not for hours of salt air, Gulf heat, and full-body exertion on the sand.

Then a coworker handed over a homemade tallow balm. Skeptical — but scientifically curious. It worked better than anything else. But it was heavy, greasy, and unrefined. The right ingredient in the wrong formula.

So the formula got rebuilt. Not the way a hobbyist experiments in a kitchen — the way someone with 15+ years of science-first professional discipline approaches a biological system. Every ingredient was researched, sourced, verified, and justified. Every percentage was calculated, not guessed. Every claim on the label was earned, not invented.

The result is St. Pete Tallow. Ancestral ingredients. Clinical precision. Built in St. Petersburg, Florida — for the people who live outside.

01 · COMMUNITY
The St. Pete Ballers Club

Over 3,200 coastal athletes. A private WhatsApp network of 600 direct members. Built around beach volleyball, physical wellness, and the social connection that happens when people move their bodies outdoors together.

02 · SCIENCE
Clinical Precision Meets Ancestral Wisdom

Fifteen-plus years in medical sales, pharma, and biologics — including surgical case support — informs every formulation decision. Tallow mirrors human sebum more closely than any plant oil on earth. Every active is cold-pressed, GC/MS verified, and IFRA compliant. Science first. Always.

03 · INTEGRITY
Every Ingredient Earns Its Place

Zero water. Zero filler. Zero synthetic silicones. Local St. Pete tallow. Sarasota beeswax. GC/MS tested essential oils. If it does not serve the skin, it does not make the formula.

THE SCIENCE

Why Tallow Works

λ
Bio-Identical Lipids

Tallow matches human sebum. The skin recognizes it, accepts it, and uses it completely — no work required.

α
CLA Rich

Grass-fed tallow is dense in Conjugated Linoleic Acid — documented anti-inflammatory and skin-barrier properties.

Ω
Fat-Soluble Vitamins

Vitamins A, D, E, and K delivered in their most bioavailable form — exactly what skin cells need for repair.

∅
Zero Dilution

Water-based products dilute every active. Our waterless formulas deliver 100% of every active directly.

THE RESEARCH

We do not make claims we cannot support.

Every ingredient in our formulas was selected based on documented biological function — not marketing trends, not anecdote, not aesthetic appeal.

The following peer-reviewed research forms the scientific foundation of our formulation decisions. We cite it not as a drug claim — but as an honest explanation of why we chose each ingredient and what the published science says about it.

These citations are provided for educational purposes. St. Pete Tallow products are cosmetics, not drugs, and are not intended to diagnose, treat, cure, or prevent any disease or condition.

01
BIO-IDENTICAL LIPIDS

Why tallow is recognized by human skin

Human sebum and bovine tallow share remarkably similar fatty acid profiles — oleic, palmitic, and stearic acids — which is why tallow integrates with the skin barrier without resistance. The skin does not have to work to absorb it.

Lampe MA et al. “Human stratum corneum lipids: characterization and regional variations.” Journal of Lipid Research, 1983. — Fluhr JW et al. “Glycerol and the skin: holistic approach to its origin and functions.” British Journal of Dermatology, 2008.

02
CONJUGATED LINOLEIC ACID

Why we source exclusively from grass-fed animals

Grass-fed tallow contains significantly higher concentrations of CLA than grain-fed sources. Published research has documented CLA as an oil-soluble compound with notable skin-barrier supporting properties. Sourcing matters — it is not a marketing distinction, it is a biochemical one.

Bhattacharya A et al. “Biological effects of conjugated linoleic acids in health and disease.” Journal of Nutritional Biochemistry, 2006. — Lin H et al. “Conjugated linoleic acid and skin barrier function.” International Journal of Molecular Sciences, 2017.

03
FAT-SOLUBLE VITAMINS A, D, E, K

Why delivery method changes everything

Vitamins A, D, E, and K are fat-soluble — meaning they require a lipid vehicle for optimal delivery to skin cells. Water-based products cannot carry them effectively. A tallow base delivers these vitamins in the exact biological medium they were designed to travel through.

Kafi R et al. “Improvement of naturally aged skin with Vitamin A.” Archives of Dermatology, 2007. — Keen MA, Hassan I. “Vitamin E in dermatology.” Indian Dermatology Online Journal, 2016.

04
COLD-PRESSED ROSEHIP SEED OIL

Why we chose rosehip as our primary active carrier oil

Rosa Canina (rosehip) seed oil is one of the most researched botanical oils in dermatology. It is naturally rich in trans-retinoic acid precursors and essential fatty acids. Published clinical research has documented its role in supporting skin appearance and texture over time.

Phetcharat L et al. “The effectiveness of a standardized rose hip powder on skin aging.” Clinical Interventions in Aging, 2015. — Ilyasov IR et al. “Physicochemical properties of rosehip seed oil.” Journal of Pharmacognosy and Phytotherapy, 2016.

05
ROSEMARY CO2 ANTIOXIDANT EXTRACT

Why we use CO2 extraction — not standard essential oil

Rosemary CO2 extract — standardized to minimum 6% carnosic acid — is one of the most effective natural antioxidant systems available for oil-based formulations. It protects the oxidation-prone fatty acids in our formula from going rancid, directly extending shelf life and maintaining active potency. Standard steam-distilled rosemary EO does not deliver the same antioxidant protection.

Oläldele OA et al. “Antioxidant properties of rosemary extract in lipid-based systems.” Food Chemistry, 2014. — Yanishlieva NV, Marinova E. “Stabilization of edible oils with natural antioxidants.” European Journal of Lipid Science and Technology, 2001.
